ACTOR Remilia 31180
{
//$Category "Touhou Characters"
  Tag "Remilia Scarlet"
  Speed 8
  FastSpeed 12
  MONSTER
  Health 2100
  damage 0
  Radius 24
  Height 64
  Scale 0.7
  MinMissileChance 160
  //MinMissileChance 3000 //I swear that this guy's coding abilities
  Mass 999999
  //MeleeThreshold 35 //were simply due to FATE
  //MeleeRange 65 //Why am I making bad touhou jokes in the comments for this
  Species SDM

  +FLOORCLIP
  +DONTFALL

  DropItem "RemiliaSpearTheGungnir"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	REMI A 0
    REMI A 1 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6042)
    REMI A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6042,4,false)
	REMI A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6042,45)	
  Idle:
    REMI BCDEFGHA 3 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
    REMI A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
    REMI ABCDEFGH 3 A_Chase
    Loop
  Pain:
    RHUR A 0 A_Pain
    RHUR ABC 3
    Goto See
  Melee:
    RMEL ABCDEF 2 A_facetarget
	RMEL G 2 A_CustomMeleeAttack(100,"touhou/remi/hit","none")
	RMEL HIJKLMNO 2
	Goto See
  Missile:
    REMI A 0 A_FaceTarget
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("UltraMode",1,"MissileUltra") //This is lunatic except faster
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"MissileLunatic")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"MissileHard")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"MissileNormal") //NO EASY MODE FOR YOU
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"MissileNormal")
    Goto MissileLunatic
  MissileNormal:
	RORB AB 3 A_FaceTarget
	RORB C 10 A_FaceTarget
	RORB DE 3 A_FaceTarget
	Goto NormalLoop
  NormalLoop:
	REMI A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire",0,0.7)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbLarge",32,0,-60,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbLarge",32,0,-30,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbLarge",32,0,60,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbLarge",32,0,30,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbMedium",32,0,67.5,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbMedium",32,0,112.5,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbMedium",32,0,-67.5,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbMedium",32,0,-112.5,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbSmall",32,0,170,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbSmall",32,0,180,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbSmall",32,0,190,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CheckSight("See")
	RORB FG 2 bright A_SetAngle(angle+4)
	Loop
  MissileHard:
	RORB AB 3 A_FaceTarget
	RORB C 10 A_FaceTarget
	RORB DE 3 A_FaceTarget
	Goto HardLoop
  HardLoop:
	REMI A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire",0,0.7)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbLarge",32,0,-120,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbLarge",32,0,-60,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbLarge",32,0,120,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbLarge",32,0,60,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbLarge",32,0,0,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbMedium",32,0,45,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbMedium",32,0,90,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbMedium",32,0,135,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbMedium",32,0,-45,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbMedium",32,0,-90,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbMedium",32,0,-135,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbSmall",32,0,160,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbSmall",32,0,180,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbSmall",32,0,200,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CheckSight("See")
	RORB FG 2 bright A_SetAngle(angle+4)

	RORB AB 3 A_FaceTarget
	RORB C 10 A_FaceTarget
	RORB DE 3 A_FaceTarget

	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbMedium",32,0,22.5,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS1OrbMedium",32,0,67.5,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)

ACTOR RemiliaNS1OrbLarge
{
  Radius 10
  Speed 18
  FastSpeed 24
  Height 20
  damage (30)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  RenderStyle Add
  DeathSound "touhou/hit2"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    RBUB A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Loop
  Death:
    RBUB AAAAAAAAAA 2 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR RemiliaSpearTheGungnir
{
//$Category "Touhou Characters"
  Tag "Remilia Scarlet"
  Speed 8
  FastSpeed 12
  MONSTER
  Health 2100
  MinMissileChance 160
  damage 0
  Radius 24
  Height 64
  Scale 0.7
  Mass 999999
  Species SDM
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +FLOORCLIP
  +DONTFALL
  +LOWGRAVITY
  //+NOGRAVITY
  //+FLOAT
  +BOSS
  +NORADIUSDMG
  +DONTMORPH
  +DONTRIP
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  +NOICEDEATH
  Seesound ""
  Deathsound "touhou/nuefire"
  Painchance 5
  Painsound "touhou/pain"
  Obituary "%o couldn't take Remilia's scarlet magic."
  HitObituary "%o was torn apart by Remilia."
  DropItem "RemiliaNS2"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	REMI A 0
	REMI A 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.05,0)
	REMI BCDEFGH 3 A_FadeIn(0.14)
  Idle:
	REMI ABCDEFGH 3 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
    REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    REMI A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	REMI ABCDEFGH 3 A_FaceTarget
    TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6043)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6043,4,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6043,40)
	RPSL B 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,26)
	RSPL B 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
	RSPL ABCDEFGHIJKLMN 3 A_FaceTarget
	RSPL A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	RSPL A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	Goto Missile
  ChaseState:
    REMI A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
    REMI ABCDEFGH 3 A_Chase
    Loop
  Pain:
    RHUR A 0 A_Pain
    RHUR ABC 3
    Goto See
  Melee:
  Missile:
    REMI A 0 A_FaceTarget
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("UltraMode",1,"MissileUltra")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"MissileLunatic")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"MissileHard")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"MissileNormal") //NO EASY MODE FOR YOU
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"MissileNormal")
    Goto MissileUltra
  MissileNormal:
	GUNG ABCDEFGHIIIIIIII 3 bright A_FaceTarget
	GUNG JJJJJJJJKL 3 bright A_CustomRailgun(0,0,"none","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",0,0,0,0,2.0,0,"HarmlessLaserTrail",-8)
	REMI A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire",0,1.0) //You better be out of the damn way by now
	REMI A 0 bright A_CustomMissile("RemiliaLaserExploderNormal",32,0,0,CMF_AIMDIRECTION) //Does exploding
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(80,0,"red","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",0,0,0,0,0,0,"RemiRedLaserTrail",-8)
	GUNG MNOP 3 bright
	GUNG P 17
	GUNG QR 3
	Goto See
  MissileHard:
	GUNG ABCDEFGHIIIIIIII 3 bright A_FaceTarget
	GUNG JJJJJJJJKL 3 bright A_CustomRailgun(0,0,"none","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",0,0,0,0,2.0,0,"HarmlessLaserTrail",-8)
	REMI A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire",0,1.0) //You better be out of the damn way by now
	REMI A 0 bright A_CustomMissile("RemiliaLaserExploderHard",32,0,0,CMF_AIMDIRECTION) //Does exploding
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(80,0,"red","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",0,0,0,0,0,0,"RemiRedLaserTrail",-8)
	GUNG MNOP 3 bright
	GUNG P 17
	GUNG QR 3
	Goto See
  MissileLunatic:
	GUNG ABCDEFGHIIIIII 3 bright A_FaceTarget

ACTOR RemiliaNS2OrbLarge
{
  Radius 12
  Speed 24
  FastSpeed 30
  Height 24
  damage (30)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  RenderStyle Add
  DeathSound "touhou/hit2"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    RBUB A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Loop
  Death:
    RBUB AAAAAAAAAA 3 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

  LoopState:
    RBL3 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Loop
  Death:
    RBL3 AAAAAAAAAA 2 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

  Death:
	RDED A 1 ACS_NamedTerminate("BHI_BossStartAttack",0)
	RDED A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStopAttack",0)

{

ACTOR RemiliaCurseKnife
{
	Speed 24
	FastSpeed 36
	Damage (10)
	Radius 8
	Height 16
	Scale 1.25
	Projectile
	-ACTIVATEIMPACT
	-ACTIVATEPCROSS
	+RIPPER
	SeeSound "touhou/fire"
	DeathSound "touhou/hit"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		KNIF A 0
		KNIF A 0 A_SetAngle(270)
	LoopState:
		KNIF A 1 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
		KNIF A 1 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("RemiliaActivationToken",1,"GiveToken")
		KNIF A 1 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
		KNIF A 1 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("RemiliaActivationToken",1,"GiveToken")
		KNIF A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaCurseOrb",0,0,0,CMF_AIMDIRECTION|CMF_TRACKOWNER)
		KNIF A 0 A_SetAngle(angle+10)
		loop
	GiveToken:
		KNIF A 7 A_GiveInventory("RemiliaActivationToken",1)
		KNIF A 0 A_Die
	Death:
		KNIF AAAAAAAAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.1)
		Stop
	}
}

		VBUB A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("RemiliaActivationToken",1,"GiveToken")
		VBUB A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaCurseOrb",0,0,0,CMF_AIMDIRECTION|CMF_TRACKOWNER)
		VBUB A 0 A_SetAngle(angle-10)
		loop
	GiveToken:
		VBUB A 4 Bright A_GiveInventory("RemiliaActivationToken",1)
		VBUB A 0 A_Die
	Death:
		VBUB AAAAAAAAAA 2 Bright A_FadeOut
		Stop
	}
}

		RBL2 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("RemiliaActivationToken",1,"StartMoving")
		RBL2 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
		Loop
	StartMoving:
		RBL2 A 0 ThrustThing(angle*256/360,6,0,0)

		RBL2 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
		Loop
	Death:
		RBL2 AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
		Stop
	}
}

ACTOR RemiliaNS4Orb
{
  Radius 3
  Speed 12
  FastSpeed 16
  Height 6
  damage (10)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  DeathSound "touhou/hit2"
  Translation "192:207=[255,0,0]:[128,0,0]","240:247=[128,0,0]:[64,0,0]"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    RRIC AA 4 Bright A_ScaleVelocity(frandom(0.5,1.5))
  LoopState:
    RRIC A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Loop
  Death:
    RRIC AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR RemiliaScarletMeister //OH GOD
{
//$Category "Touhou Characters
  Tag "Remilia Scarlet"
  Speed 8
  FastSpeed 12
  MONSTER
  Health 2000
  damage 0
  Radius 24
  Height 64
  Scale 0.7
  Mass 999999
  Species SDM
  MinMissileChance 160
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +FLOORCLIP
  +DONTFALL
  +LOWGRAVITY
  //+NOGRAVITY
  //+FLOAT
  +NEVERFAST
  +BOSS
  +NORADIUSDMG
  +DONTMORPH
  +DONTRIP
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  +NOICEDEATH
  Seesound ""
  Deathsound "touhou/nuefire"
  Painchance 2
  Painsound "touhou/pain"
  Obituary "%o couldn't take Remilia's scarlet magic."
  HitObituary "%o was torn apart by Remilia."
  DropItem "RemiliaScarletGensokyo"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	REMI A 0
	REMI A 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.05,0)
	REMI BCDEFGH 3 A_FadeIn(0.14)
  Idle:
	REMI ABCDEFGH 3 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
    REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    REMI A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	REMI ABCDEFGH 3 A_FaceTarget
    TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6049)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6049,1,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6049,30)
	RSPL B 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,29)
	RSPL B 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
	RSPL ABCDEFGHIJKLMN 3 A_FaceTarget
	RSPL A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	RSPL A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	Goto Missile
  ChaseState:
    REMI A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	REMI A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
    REMI ABCDEFGH 3 A_Chase
    Loop
  Pain:
    RHUR A 0 A_Pain
    RHUR ABC 3
    Goto See
  Melee:
  Missile:
    REMI A 0 A_FaceTarget
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("UltraMode",1,"MissileUltra")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"MissileLunatic")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"MissileHard")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"MissileNormal")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"MissileNormal")
    Goto MissileLunatic
  MissileNormal:
	RORB A 0 A_Jump(128,"MissileNormal2")
	RORB AB 3 A_FaceTarget
	RORB C 10 A_FaceTarget
	RORB DE 3 A_FaceTarget
	REMI A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire",0,0.7)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS2OrbLarge",32,0,0,CMF_OFFSETPITCH)
	REMI AAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS2OrbMedium",32,0,frandom(-10,10),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,frandom(-10,10))
	REMI AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS2OrbSmall",32,0,frandom(-20,20),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,frandom(-20,20))
	REMI A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire",0,0.7)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS2OrbLarge",32,0,45,CMF_OFFSETPITCH)
	REMI AAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS2OrbMedium",32,0,frandom(-10,10)+45,CMF_OFFSETPITCH,frandom(-10,10))
	REMI AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS2OrbSmall",32,0,frandom(-20,20)+45,CMF_OFFSETPITCH,frandom(-20,20))
	REMI A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/fire",0,0.7)
	REMI A 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS2OrbLarge",32,0,90,CMF_OFFSETPITCH)
	REMI AAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS2OrbMedium",32,0,frandom(-10,10)+90,CMF_OFFSETPITCH,frandom(-10,10))
	REMI AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("RemiliaNS2OrbSmall",32,0,frandom(-20,20)+90,CMF_OFFSETPITCH,frandom(-20,20))

ACTOR RemiliaRedMagicOrb
{
	Speed 20
	FastSpeed 20
	Damage (10)
	Radius 10
	Height 20
	Projectile
	+FORCEXYBILLBOARD
	+RIPPER
	+HEXENBOUNCE
	BounceCount 2
	SeeSound "touhou/fire"
	DeathSound "touhou/hit2"
	Renderstyle Add
	Alpha 1.0
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		VBUB A 0
		VBUB A 0 A_SetAngle(270)
	LoopState:
		VBUB A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("RemiliaActivationToken",1,"GiveToken")
		VBUB A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
		VBUB A 1 Bright A_CustomMissile("RemiliaFinalOrb",0,0,0,CMF_AIMDIRECTION|CMF_TRACKOWNER)
		VBUB A 1 Bright A_SetAngle(angle+10)
		loop
	GiveToken:
		VBUB A 8 Bright A_GiveInventory("RemiliaActivationToken",1)
		VBUB A 0 A_Die
	Death:
		VBUB AAAAAAAAAA 2 Bright A_FadeOut
		Stop
	}
}

ACTOR RemiliaFinalOrb
{
	Speed 0
	FastSpeed 0
	Damage (10)
	Radius 4
	Height 8
	Projectile
	+FORCEXYBILLBOARD
	SeeSound ""
	DeathSound "touhou/hit"
	Renderstyle Add
	Alpha 1.0
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		RBL2 A 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("RemiliaActivationToken",1,"StartMoving")
		RBL2 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
		Loop
	StartMoving:
		RBL2 A 0 ThrustThing(angle*256/360,7,0,0)
	LoopState:
		RBL2 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
		Loop
	Death:
		RBL2 AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
		Stop
	}
}
